52→\n    53→bool Utility::labelWildcardMatch(absl::string_view dns_label, absl::string_view pattern) {\n    54→  constexpr char glob = '*';\n    55→  // Check the special case of a single * pattern, as it's common.\n    56→  if (pattern.size() == 1 && pattern[0] == glob) {\n    57→    return true;\n    58→  }\n    59→  // Only valid if wildcard character appear once.\n    60→  if (std::count(pattern.begin(), pattern.end(), glob) == 1) {\n    61→    std::vector<absl::string_view> split_pattern = absl::StrSplit(pattern, glob);\n    62→    return (pattern.size() <= dns_label.size() + 1) &&\n    63→           absl::StartsWith(dns_label, split_pattern[0]) &&\n    64→           absl::EndsWith(dns_label, split_pattern[1]);\n    65→  }\n    66→  return false;\n    67→}\n    68→\n    69→bool Utility::dnsNameMatch(absl::string_view dns_name, absl::string_view pattern) {\n    70→  // A-label ACE prefix https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc5890#section-2.3.2.5.\n    71→  constexpr absl::string_view ACE_prefix = \"xn--\";\n    72→  const std::string lower_case_dns_name = absl::AsciiStrToLower(dns_name);\n    73→  const std::string lower_case_pattern = absl::AsciiStrToLower(pattern);\n    74→  if (lower_case_dns_name == lower_case_pattern) {\n    75→    return true;\n    76→  }\n    77→\n    78→  std::vector<absl::string_view> split_pattern =\n    79→      absl::StrSplit(lower_case_pattern, absl::MaxSplits('.', 1));\n    80→  std::vector<absl::string_view> split_dns_name =\n    81→      absl::StrSplit(lower_case_dns_name, absl::MaxSplits('.', 1));\n    82→\n    83→  // dns name and pattern should contain more than 1 label to match.\n    84→  if (split_pattern.size() < 2 || split_dns_name.size() < 2) {\n    85→    return false;\n    86→  }\n    87→  // Only the left-most label in the pattern contains wildcard '*' and is not an A-label.\n    88→  if ((split_pattern[0].find('*') != absl::string_view::npos) &&\n    89→      (split_pattern[1].find('*') == absl::string_view::npos) &&\n    90→      (!absl::StartsWith(split_pattern[0], ACE_prefix))) {\n    91→    return (split_dns_name[1] == split_pattern[1]) &&\n    92→           labelWildcardMatch(split_dns_name[0], split_pattern[0]);\n    93→  }\n    94→\n    95→  return false;\n    96→}\n    97→\n    98→namespace {\n    99→\n   100→enum class CertName { Issuer, Subject };\n   101→\n   102→/**\n   103→ * Retrieves a name from a certificate and formats it as an RFC 2253 name.\n   104→ * @param cert the certificate.\n   105→ * @param desired_name the desired getRFC2253NameFromCertificate(X509& cert, CertName desired_name) {\n   109→  bssl::UniquePtr<BIO> buf(BIO_new(BIO_s_mem()));\n   110→  RELEASE_ASSERT(buf != nullptr, \"\");\n   111→\n   112→ 118→    name = X509_get_subject_name(&cert);\n   119→    break;\n   120→  }\n   121→\n   122→  // flags=XN_FLAG_RFC2253 is the documented parameter for single-line output in RFC 2253 format.\n   123→  // Example from the RFC:\n   124→  //   * Single value per Relative Distinguished Name (RDN): CN=Steve Kille,O=Isode Limited,C=GB\n   125→  //   * Multivalue output in first RDN: OU=Sales+CN=J. Smith,O=Widget Inc.,C=US\n   126→  //   * Quoted comma in Organization: CN=L. = BIO_mem_contents(buf.get(), &data, &data_len);\n   132→  ASSERT(rc == 1);\n   133→  return {reinterpret_cast<const char*>(data), data_len};\n   134→}\n   135→\n   136→} // namespace\n   137→\n Example of config.cipherSuites():\n   120→      // \"-ALL:[ECDHE-ECDSA-AES128-GCM-SHA256|ECDHE-ECDSA-CHACHA20-POLY1305]:ECDHE-ECDSA-AES128-SHA\".\n   121→      //\n   122→      // \"-\" is both an operator when in the leading position of a token (-ALL: don't allow this\n   123→      // cipher), and the common separator in names (ECDHE-ECDSA-AES128-GCM-SHA256). Don't split on\n   124→      // it because it will separate pieces of the same cipher. When it is a leading character, it\n   125→      // is removed below.\n   126→      std::vector<absl::string_view> ciphers =\n   127→          StringUtil::splitToken(config.cipherSuites(), \":+![|]\", false);\n   128→      std::vector<std::string> bad_ciphers;\n   129→      for (const auto& cipher : ciphers) {\n   130→        std::string cipher_str(cipher);\n   131→\n   132→        if (absl::StartsWith(cipher_str, \"-\")) {\n   133→          cipher_str.erase(cipher_str.begin());\n   134→        }\n   135→\n   136→        if (!SSL_CTX_set_strict_cipher_list(ctx.ssl_ctx_.get(), cipher_str.c_str())) {\n   137→          bad_ciphers.push_back(cipher_str);\n   138→        }\n   139→      }\n   140→      creation_status = absl::InvalidArgumentError(\n   141→          fmt::format(\"Failed to initialize cipher suites {}. The following \"\n   142→                      \"ciphers were rejected when tried individually: {}\",\n   143→                      config.cipherSuites(), absl::StrJoin(bad_ciphers, \", \")));\n   144→      return;\n   145→    }\n   146→\n   147→    if (!capabilities_.provides_ciphers_and_curves &&\n   148→        !SSL_CTX_set1_curves_list(ctx.ssl_ctx_.get(), config.ecdhCurves().c_str())) {\n   149→      creation_status = absl::InvalidArgumentError(\n   150→          absl::StrCat(\"Failed to initialize ECDH curves \", config.ecdhCurves()));\n   151→      return;\n   152→    }\n   153→\n   154→    // Set signature algorithms if given, otherwise fall back to BoringSSL defaults.\n   155→    if (!capabilities_.provides_sigalgs && !config.signatureAlgorithms().empty()) {\n   156→      if (!SSL_CTX_set1_sigalgs_list(ctx.ssl_ctx_.get(), config.signatureAlgorithms().c_str())) {\n   157→        creation_status = absl::InvalidArgumentError(absl::StrCat(\n   158→            \"Failed to initialize TLS signature algorithms \", config.signatureAlgorithms()));\n   159→        return;\n   160→      }\n   161→    }\n   162→  }\n   163→\n   164→  auto verify_mode_or_error = cert_validator_->initializeSslContexts(\n   165→      ssl_contexts, config.capabilities().provides_certificates);\n   166→  SET_AND_RETURN_IF_NOT_OK(verify_mode_or_error.status(), creation_status);\n   167→  auto verify_mode = verify_mode_or_error.value();\n   168→\n   169→  if (!capabilities_.verifies_peer_certificates) {\n   170→    for (auto ctx : ssl_contexts) {\n   171→      if (verify_mode != SSL_VERIFY_NONE) {\n   172→        // TODO(danzh) Envoy's use of SSL_VERIFY_NONE does not quite match the actual semantics as\n   173→        // a client. As a client, SSL_VERIFY_NONE means to verify the certificate (which will fail\n   174→        // without trust anchors), save the result in the session ticket, but otherwise continue\n   175→        // with the handshake. But Envoy actually wants it to accept all certificates. The\n   176→        // disadvantage of using SSL_VERIFY_NONE is that it records the verify_result, which Envoy\n   177→        // never queries but gets saved in session tickets, and tries to find an anchor that isn't\n   178→        // there. And also it differs from server side behavior of SSL_VERIFY_NONE which won't\n   179→        // even request client certs. So, instead, we should configure a callback to skip\n   180→        // validation and always supply the callback to boring SSL.\n   181→        SSL_CTX_set_custom_verify(ctx, verify_mode, customVerifyCallback);\n   182→        SSL_CTX_set_reverify_on_resume(ctx, /*reverify_on_resume_enabled)=*/1);\n   183→      }\n   184→    }\n   185→  }\n   186→\n   187→#ifdef BORINGSSL_FIPS\n   188→  if (!capabilities_.is_fips_compliant) {\n   189→    creation_status = absl::InvalidArgumentError(\n   190→        \"Can't load a FIPS noncompliant custom handshaker while running in FIPS compliant mode.\");\n   191→    return;\n   192→  }\n   193→#endif\n   194→\n   195→  if (!capabilities_.provides_certificates) {\n   196→    for (uint32_t i = 0; i < tls_certificates.size(); ++i) {\n   197→      auto& ctx = tls_contexts_[i];\n   198→      // Load certificate chain.\n   199→      const auto& tls_certificate = tls_certificates[i].get();\n   200→      if (!tls_certificate.pkcs12().empty()) {\n   201→        creation_status = ctx.loadPkcs12(tls_certificate.pkcs12(), tls_certificate.pkcs12Path(),\n   202→                                         tls_certificate.password());\n   203→      } else {\n   204→        creation_status = ctx.loadCertificateChain(tls_certificate.certificateChain(),\n   205→                                                   tls_certificate.certificateChainPath());\n   206→      }\n   207→      if (!creation_status.ok()) {\n   208→        return;\n   209→      }\n   210→      // The must staple extension means the certificate promises to carry\n   211→      // with it an OCSP staple. https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7633#section-6\n   212→      constexpr absl::string_view tls_feature_ext = \"1.3.6.1.5.5.7.1.24\";\n   213→      constexpr absl::string_view must_staple_ext_value = \"\\x30\\x3\\x02\\x01\\x05\";\n   214→      auto must_staple = Utility::getCertificateExtensionValue(*ctx.cert_chain_, tls_feature_ext);\n   215→      if (must_staple == must_staple_ext_value) {\n   216→        ctx.is_must_staple_ = true;\n   217→      }\n   218→\n   219→      bssl::UniquePtr<EVP_PKEY> public_key(X509_get_pubkey(ctx.cert_chain_.get()));\n   220→      const int pkey_id = EVP_PKEY_id(public_key.get());\n   221→      ctx.is_ecdsa_ = pkey_id == EVP_PKEY_EC;\n   222→      switch (pkey_id) {\n   223→      case EVP_PKEY_EC: {\n   224→        // We only support P-256 ECDSA today.\n   225→        const EC_KEY* ecdsa_public_key = EVP_PKEY_get0_EC_KEY(public_key.get());\n   226→        // Since we checked the key type above, this should be valid.\n   227→        ASSERT(ecdsa_public_key != nullptr);\n   228→        const EC_GROUP* ecdsa_group = EC_KEY_get0_group(ecdsa_public_key);\n   229→        if (ecdsa_group == nullptr ||\n   230→            EC_GROUP_get_curve_name(ecdsa_group) != NID_X9_62_prime256v1) {\n   231→          creation_status = absl::InvalidArgumentError(\n   232→              fmt::format(\"Failed to load certificate chain from {}, only P-256 \"\n   233→                          \"ECDSA certificates are supported\",\n   234→                          ctx.cert_chain_file_path_));\n   235→          return;\n   236→        }\n   237→        ctx.is_ecdsa_ = true;\n   238→      } break;\n   239→      case EVP_PKEY_RSA: {\n   240→        // We require RSA certificates with 2048-bit or larger keys.\n   241→        const RSA* rsa_public_key = EVP_PKEY_get0_RSA(public_key.get());\n   242→        // Since we checked the key type above, this should be valid.\n   243→        ASSERT(rsa_public_key != nullptr);\n   244→        const unsigned rsa_key_length = RSA_bits(rsa_public_key);\n   245→#ifdef BORINGSSL_FIPS\n   246→        if (rsa_key_length != 2048 && rsa_key_length != 3072 && rsa_key_length != 4096) {\n   247→          creation_status = absl::InvalidArgumentError(\n   248→              fmt::format(\"Failed to load certificate chain from {}, only RSA certificates with \"\n   249→                          \"2048-bit, 3072-bit or 4096-bit keys are supported in FIPS mode\",\n   250→                          ctx.cert_chain_file_path_));\n   251→          return;\n   252→        }\n   253→#else\n   254→        if (rsa_key_length < 2048) {\n   255→          creation_status = absl::InvalidArgumentError(\n   256→              fmt::format(\"Failed to load certificate chain from {}, only RSA \"\n   257→                          \"certificates with 2048-bit or larger keys are supported\",\n   258→                          ctx.cert_chain_file_path_));\n   259→          return;\n   260→        }\n   261→#endif\n   262→      } break;\n   263→#ifdef BORINGSSL_FIPS\n   264→      default:\n   265→        creation_status = absl::InvalidArgumentError(\n   266→            fmt::format(\"Failed to load certificate chain from {}, only RSA and \"\n   267→                        \"ECDSA certificates are supported in FIPS mode\",\n   268→                        ctx.cert_chain_file_path_));\n   269→        return;\n   270→#endif\n   271→      }\n   272→\n   273→      Envoy::Ssl::PrivateKeyMethodProviderSharedPtr private_key_method_provider =\n   274→          tls_certificate.privateKeyMethod();\n   275→      // We either have a private key or a BoringSSL private key method provider.\n   276→      if (private_key_method_provider) {\n   277→        ctx.private_key_method_provider_ = private_key_method_provider;\n   278→        // The provider has a reference to the private key method for the context lifetime.\n   279→        Ssl::BoringSslPrivateKeyMethodSharedPtr private_key_method =\n   280→            private_key_method_provider->getBoringSslPrivateKeyMethod();\n   281→        if (private_key_method == nullptr) {\n   282→          creation_status = absl::InvalidArgumentError(\n   283→              fmt::format(\"Failed to get BoringSSL private key method from provider\"));\n   284→          return;\n   285→        }\n   286→#ifdef BORINGSSL_FIPS\n   287→        if (!ctx.private_key_method_provider_->checkFips()) {\n   288→          creation_status = absl::InvalidArgumentError(\n   289→              fmt::format(\"Private key method doesn't support FIPS mode with current parameters\"));\n   290→          return;\n   291→        }\n   292→#endif\n   293→        SSL_CTX_set_private_key_method(ctx.ssl_ctx_.get(), private_key_method.get());\n   294→      } else if (!tls_certificate.privateKey().empty()) {\n   295→        // Load private key.\n   296→        creation_status =\n   297→            ctx.loadPrivateKey(tls_certificate.privateKey(), tls_certificate.privateKeyPath(),\n   298→                               tls_certificate.password());\n   299→        if (!creation_status.ok()) {\n   300→          return;\n   301→        }\n   302→      }\n   303→\n   304→      if (additional_init != nullptr) {\n   305→        absl::Status init_status = additional_init(ctx, tls_certificate);\n   306→        SET_AND_RETURN_IF_NOT_OK(creation_status, init_status);\n   307→      }\n   308→    }\n   309→  }\n   310→\n   311→  // use the server's cipher list preferences\n   312→  for (auto& ctx : tls_contexts_) {\n   313→    SSL_CTX_set_options(ctx.ssl_ctx_.get(), SSL_OP_CIPHER_SERVER_PREFERENCE);\n   314→  }\n   315→\n   316→  parsed_alpn_protocols_ = parseAlpnProtocols(config.alpnProtocols(), creation_status);\n   317→  SET_AND_RETURN_IF_NOT_OK(creation_status, creation_status);\n   318→\n   319→#if BORINGSSL_API_VERSION >= 21\n   320→  //   323→  stat_name_set_->rememberBuiltins(list);\n   324→\n   325→  list.resize(SSL_get_all_curve_names(nullptr, 0));\n   326→  SSL_get_all_curve_names(list.data(), list.size());\n   327→  stat_name_set_->rememberBuiltins(list);\n   328→\n   329→  list.resize(SSL_get_all_signature_algorithm_names(nullptr, 0));\n   330→  SSL_get_all_signature_algorithm_names(list.data(), list.size());\n   331→  stat_name_set_->rememberBuiltins(list);\n   332→\n   333→  list.resize(SSL_get_all_version_names(nullptr, 0));\n   334→  SSL_get_all_version_names(list.data(), list.size());\n   335→  stat_name_set_->rememberBuiltins(list);\n   336→#else\n   337→  // Use the SSL library to iterate over the configured ciphers.\n   338→  //\n   339→  // Note that if a negotiated cipher suite is outside of this set, we'll issue an ENVOY_BUG.\n   340→  for (Ssl::TlsContext& tls_context : tls_contexts_) {\n   341→    for (const SSL_CIPHER* cipher : SSL_CTX_get_ciphers(tls_context.ssl_ctx_.get())) {\n   342→      stat_name_set_->rememberBuiltin(SSL_CIPHER_get_name(cipher));\n   343→    }\n   344→  }\n   345→\n   346→  // Add supported cipher suites from the TLS 1.3 spec:\n   347→  // https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc8446#appendix-B.4\n   348→  // AES-CCM cipher suites are removed (no BoringSSL support).\n   349→  //\n   350→  // Note that if a negotiated cipher suite is outside of this set, we'll issue an ENVOY_BUG.\n   351→  stat_name_set_->rememberBuiltins(\n   352→      {\"TLS_AES_128_GCM_SHA256\", \"TLS_AES_256_GCM_SHA384\", Source:\n   361→  // https://github.com/google/boringssl/blob/3743aafdacff2f7b083615a043a37101f740fa53/ssl/ssl_privkey.cc#L436-L453\n   362→  //\n   363→  // Note that if a negotiated algorithm is outside of this set, we'll issue an ENVOY_BUG.\n   364→  stat_name_set_->rememberBuiltins({\n   365→      \"rsa_pkcs1_md5_sha1\",\n   366→      \"rsa_pkcs1_sha1\",\n   367→      \"rsa_pkcs1_sha256\",\n   368→      \"rsa_pkcs1_sha384\",\n   369→      \"rsa_pkcs1_sha512\",\n   370→      \"ecdsa_sha1\",\n   371→      \"ecdsa_secp256r1_sha256\",\n   372→      \"ecdsa_secp384r1_sha384\",\n   373→      \"ecdsa_secp521r1_sha512\",\n   374→      \"rsa_pss_rsae_sha256\",\n   375→      \"rsa_pss_rsae_sha384\",\n   376→      \"rsa_pss_rsae_sha512\",\n   377→      \"ed25519\",\n   378→  });\n   379→\n   380→  // All supported protocol versions.\n   381→  //\n   382→  // Note that if a negotiated version is outside of this set, we'll issue an ENVOY_BUG.\n   383→   387→  // SSL_CTX, if set.\n   388→  if (auto sslctx_cb = config.sslctxCb(); sslctx_cb) {\n   389→    for (Ssl::TlsContext& ctx : tls_contexts_) {\n   390→      sslctx_cb(ctx.ssl_ctx_.get());\n   391→    }\n   392→  }\n   393→\n   394→  if (!config.tlsKeyLogPath().empty()) {\n   395→    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Enable tls key log\");\n   396→    auto file_or_error = SET_AND_RETURN_IF_NOT_OK(file_or_error.status(), creation_status);\n   399→    tls_keylog_file_ = file_or_error.value();\n   400→    for (auto& context : tls_contexts_) {\n   401→      SSL_CTX* ctx = ContextImpl::keylogCallback(const SSL* ssl, const char* line) {\n   409→  ASSERT(ssl != nullptr);\n   410→  auto callbacks =\n   411→      static_cast<Network::TransportSocketCallbacks*>(SSL_get_ex_data(ssl, sslSocketIndex()));\n   412→  auto ctx = static_cast<ContextImpl*>(SSL_CTX_get_app_data(SSL_get_SSL_CTX(ssl)));\n   413→  ASSERT(callbacks != nullptr);\n   414→  ASSERT(ctx != nullptr);\n   415→\n   416→  if ((ctx->tls_keylog_local_.getIpListSize() == 0 ||\n   417→       ctx->tls_keylog_local_.contains(\n   418→    *(callbacks->connection().connectionInfoProvider().remoteAddress())))) {\n   422→    ctx->tls_keylog_file_->write(absl::StrCat(line, \"\\n\"));\n   423→  }\n   424→}\n   425→\n   426→int ContextImpl::sslSocketIndex() {\n   427→  CONSTRUCT_ON_FIRST_USE(int, []() -> int {\n   428→    int ssl_socket_index = SSL_get_ex_new_index(0, nullptr, nullptr, nullptr, nullptr);\n   429→    RELEASE_ASSERT(ssl_socket_index >= 0, \"\");\n   430→    return ssl_socket_index;\n   431→  }());\n   432→}\n   433→\n   434→std::vector<uint8_t> ContextImpl::parseAlpnProtocols(const std::string& alpn_protocols,\n   435→                                                     absl::Status& parse_status) {\n   436→  if (alpn_protocols.empty()) {\n   437→    return {};\n   438→  }\n   439→\n   440→  if (alpn_protocols.size() >= 65535) {\n   441→    parse_status = absl::InvalidArgumentError(\"Invalid ALPN protocol string\");\n   442→    return {};\n   443→  }\n   444→\n   445→  std::vector<uint8_t> out(alpn_protocols.size() + 1);\n   446→  size_t start = 0;\n   447→  for (size_t i = 0; i <= alpn_protocols.size(); i++) {\n   448→    if (i == alpn_protocols.size() || }\n   453→\n   454→      out[start] = i - start;\n   455→      start = i + 1;\n   456→    } else {\n   457→      out[i + 1] = alpn_protocols[i];\n   458→    }\n   459→  }\n   460→\n   461→  return out;\n   462→}\n   463→\n   464→absl::StatusOr<bssl::UniquePtr<SSL>>\n   465→ContextImpl::newSsl(const Network::TransportSocketOptionsConstSharedPtr& options) {\n   466→  // We use the first 473→\n   474→enum ssl_verify_result_t ContextImpl::customVerifyCallback(SSL* ssl, uint8_t* out_alert) {\n   475→  auto* extended_socket_info = reinterpret_cast<Envoy::Ssl::SslExtendedSocketInfo*>(\n   476→      SSL_get_ex_data(ssl, ContextImpl::sslExtendedSocketInfoIndex()));\n   477→  if (extended_socket_info->certificateValidationResult() != Ssl::ValidateStatus::NotStarted) {\n   478→    if (extended_socket_info->certificateValidationResult() == Ssl::ValidateStatus::Pending) {\n   479→      return ssl_verify_retry;\n   480→    }\n   481→    ENVOY_LOG(trace, \"Already has a result: {}\",\n   482→              static_cast<int>(extended_socket_info->certificateValidationStatus()));\n   483→    // Already has a binary result, return immediately.\n   484→    *out_alert = 487→               : ssl_verify_invalid;\n   488→  }\n   489→  // Hasn't kicked off any validation for this connection yet.\n   490→  SSL_CTX* ssl_ctx = SSL_get_SSL_CTX(ssl);\n   491→  ContextImpl* context_impl = static_cast<ContextImpl*>(SSL_CTX_get_app_data(ssl_ctx));\n   492→  auto transport_socket_options_shared_ptr_ptr =\n   493→      static_cast<const Network::TransportSocketOptionsConstSharedPtr*>(SSL_get_app_data(ssl));\n   494→  ASSERT(transport_socket_options_shared_ptr_ptr);\n   495→  ValidationResults result = ValidationResults::ValidationStatus::Successful:\n   499→    return ssl_verify_ok;\n   500→  case ValidationResults::ValidationStatus::Pending:\n   501→    return ssl_verify_retry;\n   502→  case ValidationResults::ValidationStatus::Failed: {\n   503→    if (result.tls_alert.has_value() && out_alert) {\n   504→      *out_alert = result.tls_alert.value();\n   505→    }\n   506→    return ssl_verify_invalid;\n   507→  }\n   508→  }\n   509→  PANIC(\"not reached\");\n   510→}\n   511→\n   512→ValidationResults ContextImpl::customVerifyCertChain(\n   513→ Stats::Utility::counterFromElements(scope_, {name, value_stat_name}).inc();\n   549→}\n   550→\n   551→void ContextImpl::logHandshake(SSL* ssl) const {\n   552→  stats_.handshake_.inc();\n   553→\n   554→  if (SSL_session_reused(ssl)) {\n   555→    stats_.session_reused_.inc();\n   556→  }\n   557→\n   558→  incCounter(ssl_ciphers_, SSL_get_cipher_name(ssl), unknown_ssl_cipher_);\n   559→                                 tls_certificate.password());\n      } else {\n        creation_status = ctx.loadCertificateChain(tls_certificate.certificateChain(),\n                                                   tls_certificate.certificateChainPath());\n      }\n      if (!creation_status.ok()) {\n        return;\n      }\n      // The must staple extension means the certificate promises to carry\n      // with it an OCSP staple. https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7633#section-6\n      constexpr absl::string_view tls_feature_ext = \"1.3.6.1.5.5.7.1.24\";\n      constexpr absl::string_view must_staple_ext_value = \"\\x30\\x3\\x02\\x01\\x05\";\n      auto must_staple = Utility::getCertificateExtensionValue(*ctx.cert_chain_, tls_feature_ext);\n      if (must_staple == must_staple_ext_value) {\n        ctx.is_must_staple_ = true;\n      }\n\n      bssl::UniquePtr<EVP_PKEY> public_key(X509_get_pubkey(ctx.cert_chain_.get()));\n      const int pkey_id = EVP_PKEY_id(public_key.get());\n      ctx.is_ecdsa_ = pkey_id == EVP_PKEY_EC;\n      switch (pkey_id) {\n      case EVP_PKEY_EC: {\n        // We only support P-256 ECDSA today.\n        const EC_KEY* ecdsa_public_key = EVP_PKEY_get0_EC_KEY(public_key.get());\n        // Since we checked the key type above, this should be valid.\n        ASSERT(ecdsa_public_key != nullptr);\n        const EC_GROUP* ecdsa_group = EC_KEY_get0_group(ecdsa_public_key);\n        if (ecdsa_group == nullptr ||\n            EC_GROUP_get_curve_name(ecdsa_group) != NID_X9_62_prime256v1) {\n          creation_status = absl::InvalidArgumentError(\n              fmt::format(\"Failed to load certificate chain from {}, only P-256 \"\n                          \"ECDSA certificates are supported\",\n                          ctx.cert_chain_file_path_));\n          return;\n        }\n        ctx.is_ecdsa_ = true;\n      } break;\n      case EVP_PKEY_RSA: {\n        // We require RSA certificates with 2048-bit or larger keys.\n        const RSA* rsa_public_key = EVP_PKEY_get0_RSA(public_key.get());\n        // Since we checked the key type above, this should be valid.\n        ASSERT(rsa_public_key != nullptr);\n        const unsigned rsa_key_length = RSA_bits(rsa_public_key);\n#ifdef BORINGSSL_FIPS\n        if (rsa_key_length != 2048 && rsa_key_length != 3072 && rsa_key_length != 4096) {\n          creation_status = absl::InvalidArgumentError(\n              fmt::format(\"Failed to load certificate chain from {}, only RSA certificates with \"\n                          \"2048-bit, 3072-bit or 4096-bit keys are supported in FIPS mode\",\n                          ctx.cert_chain_file_path_));\n          return;\n        }\n#else\n        if (rsa_key_length < 2048) {\n          creation_status = absl::InvalidArgumentError(\n              fmt::format(\"Failed to load certificate chain from {}, only RSA \"\n                          \"certificates with 2048-bit or larger keys are supported\",\n                          ctx.cert_chain_file_path_));\n          return;\n        }\n#endif\n      } break;\n#ifdef BORINGSSL_FIPS\n      default:\n        creation_status = absl::InvalidArgumentError(\n            fmt::format(\"Failed to load certificate chain from {}, only RSA and \"\n                        \"ECDSA certificates are supported in FIPS mode\",\n                        ctx.cert_chain_file_path_));\n        return;\n#endif\n      }\n\n      Envoy::Ssl::PrivateKeyMethodProviderSharedPtr private_key_method_provider =\n          tls_certificate.privateKeyMethod();\n      // We either have a private key or a BoringSSL private key method provider.\n      if (private_key_method_provider) {\n        ctx.private_key_method_provider_ = private_key_method_provider;\n        // The provider has a reference to the private key method for the context lifetime.\n        Ssl::BoringSslPrivateKeyMethodSharedPtr private_key_method =\n            private_key_method_provider->getBoringSslPrivateKeyMethod();\n        if (private_key_method == nullptr) {\n          creation_status = absl::InvalidArgumentError(\n              fmt::format(\"Failed to get BoringSSL private key method from provider\"));\n          return;\n        }\n#ifdef BORINGSSL_FIPS\n        if (!ctx.private_key_method_provider_->checkFips()) {\n          creation_status = absl::InvalidArgumentError(\n              fmt::format(\"Private key method doesn't support FIPS mode with current parameters\"));\n          return;\n        }\n#endif\n        SSL_CTX_set_private_key_method(ctx.ssl_ctx_.get(), private_key_method.get());\n      } else if (!tls_certificate.privateKey().empty()) {\n        // Load private key.\n        creation_status =\n            ctx.loadPrivateKey(tls_certificate.privateKey(), tls_certificate.privateKeyPath(),\n                               tls_certificate.password());\n        if (!creation_status.ok()) {\n          return;\n        }\n      }\n\n      if (additional_init != nullptr) {\n        absl::Status init_status = additional_init(ctx, tls_certificate);\n        SET_AND_RETURN_IF_NOT_OK(creation_status, init_status);\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  // use the server's cipher list preferences\n  for (auto& ctx : tls_contexts_) {\n    SSL_CTX_set_options(ctx.ssl_ctx_.get(), SSL_OP_CIPHER_SERVER_PREFERENCE);\n  }\n\n  parsed_alpn_protocols_ = parseAlpnProtocols(config.alpnProtocols(), creation_status);\n  SET_AND_RETURN_IF_NOT_OK(creation_status, creation_status);\n\n#if BORINGSSL_API_VERSION >= 21\n  // Register stat names based on lists reported by BoringSSL.\n  std::vector<const char*> list(SSL_get_all_cipher_names(nullptr, 0));\n  SSL_get_all_cipher_names(list.data(), list.size());\n  stat_name_set_->rememberBuiltins(list);\n\n  list.resize(SSL_get_all_curve_names(nullptr, 0));\n  SSL_get_all_curve_names(list.data(), list.size());\n  stat_name_set_->rememberBuiltins(list);\n\n  list.resize(SSL_get_all_signature_algorithm_names(nullptr, 0));\n  SSL_get_all_signature_algorithm_names(list.data(), list.size());\n  stat_name_set_->rememberBuiltins(list);\n\n  list.resize(SSL_get_all_version_names(nullptr, 0));\n  SSL_get_all_version_names(list.data(), list.size());\n  stat_name_set_->rememberBuiltins(list);\n#else\n  // Use the SSL library to iterate over the configured ciphers.\n  //\n  // Note that if a negotiated cipher suite is outside of this set, we'll issue an ENVOY_BUG.\n  for (Ssl::TlsContext& tls_context : tls_contexts_) {\n    for (const SSL_CIPHER* cipher : SSL_CTX_get_ciphers(tls_context.ssl_ctx_.get())) {\n      stat_name_set_->rememberBuiltin(SSL_CIPHER_get_name(cipher));\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Add supported cipher suites from the TLS 1.3 spec:\n  // https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc8446#appendix-B.4\n  // AES-CCM cipher suites are removed (no BoringSSL support).\n  //\n  // Note that if a negotiated cipher suite is outside of this set, we'll issue an ENVOY_BUG.\n  stat_name_set_->rememberBuiltins(\n      {\"TLS_AES_128_GCM_SHA256\", \"TLS_AES_256_GCM_SHA384\", \"TLS_CHACHA20_POLY1305_SHA256\"});\n\n  // All supported curves. Source:\n  // https://github.com/google/boringssl/blob/3743aafdacff2f7b083615a043a37101f740fa53/ssl/ssl_key_share.cc#L302-L309\n  //\n  // Note that if a negotiated curve is outside of this set, we'll issue an ENVOY_BUG.\n  stat_name_set_->rememberBuiltins({\"P-224\", \"P-256\", \"P-384\", \"P-521\", \"X25519\", \"CECPQ2\"});\n\n  // All supported signature algorithms. Source:\n  // https://github.com/google/boringssl/blob/3743aafdacff2f7b083615a043a37101f740fa53/ssl/ssl_privkey.cc#L436-L453\n  //\n  // Note that if a negotiated algorithm is outside of this set, we'll issue an ENVOY_BUG.\n  stat_name_set_->rememberBuiltins({\n      \"rsa_pkcs1_md5_sha1\",\n      \"rsa_pkcs1_sha1\",\n      \"rsa_pkcs1_sha256\",\n      \"rsa_pkcs1_sha384\",\n      \"rsa_pkcs1_sha512\",\n      \"ecdsa_sha1\",\n      \"ecdsa_secp256r1_sha256\",\n      \"ecdsa_secp384r1_sha384\",\n      \"ecdsa_secp521r1_sha512\",\n      \"rsa_pss_rsae_sha256\",\n      \"rsa_pss_rsae_sha384\",\n      \"rsa_pss_rsae_sha512\",\n      \"ed25519\",\n  });\n\n  // All supported protocol versions.\n  //\n  // Note that if a negotiated version is outside of this set, we'll issue an ENVOY_BUG.\n  stat_name_set_->rememberBuiltins({\"TLSv1\", \"TLSv1.1\", \"TLSv1.2\", \"TLSv1.3\"});\n#endif\n\n  // As late as possible, run the custom SSL_CTX configuration callback on each\n  // SSL_CTX, if set.\n  if (auto sslctx_cb = config.sslctxCb(); sslctx_cb) {\n    for (Ssl::TlsContext& ctx : tls_contexts_) {\n      sslctx_cb(ctx.ssl_ctx_.get());\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (!config.tlsKeyLogPath().empty()) {\n    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Enable tls key log\");\n    auto file_or_error = config.accessLogManager().createAccessLog(\n        Filesystem::FilePathAndType{Filesystem::DestinationType::File, config.tlsKeyLogPath()});\n    SET_AND_RETURN_IF_NOT_OK(file_or_error.status(), creation_status);\n    tls_keylog_file_ = file_or_error.value();\n    for (auto& context : tls_contexts_) {\n      SSL_CTX* ctx = context.ssl_ctx_.get();\n      ASSERT(ctx != nullptr);\n      SSL_CTX_set_keylog_callback(ctx, keylogCallback);\n    }\n  }\n}\n\nvoid ContextImpl::keylogCallback(const SSL* ssl, const char* line) {\n  ASSERT(ssl != nullptr);\n  auto callbacks =\n      static_cast<Network::TransportSocketCallbacks*>(SSL_get_ex_data(ssl, sslSocketIndex()));\n  auto ctx = static_cast<ContextImpl*>(SSL_CTX_get_app_data(SSL_get_SSL_CTX(ssl)));\n  ASSERT(callbacks != nullptr);\n  ASSERT(ctx != nullptr);\n\n  if ((ctx->tls_keylog_local_.getIpListSize() == 0 ||\n       ctx->tls_keylog_local_.contains(\n           *(callbacks->connection().connectionInfoProvider().localAddress()))) &&\n      (ctx->tls_keylog_remote_.getIpListSize() == 0 ||\n       ctx->tls_keylog_remote_.contains(\n           *(callbacks->connection().connectionInfoProvider().remoteAddress())))) {\n    ctx->tls_keylog_file_->write(absl::StrCat(line, \"\\n\"));\n  }\n}\n\nint ContextImpl::sslSocketIndex() {\n  CONSTRUCT_ON_FIRST_USE(int, []() -> int {\n    int ssl_socket_index = SSL_get_ex_new_index(0, nullptr, nullptr, nullptr, nullptr);\n    RELEASE_ASSERT(ssl_socket_index >= 0, \"\");\n    return ssl_socket_index;\n  }());\n}\n\nstd::vector<uint8_t> ContextImpl::parseAlpnProtocols(const std::string& alpn_protocols,\n                                                     absl::Status& parse_status) {\n  if (alpn_protocols.empty()) {\n    return {};\n  }\n\n  if (alpn_protocols.size() >= 65535) {\n    parse_status = absl::InvalidArgumentError(\"Invalid ALPN protocol string\");\n    return {};\n  }\n\n  std::vector<uint8_t> out(alpn_protocols.size() + 1);\n  size_t start = 0;\n  for (size_t i = 0; i <= alpn_protocols.size(); i++) {\n    if (i == alpn_protocols.size() || alpn_protocols[i] == ',') {\n      if (i - start > 255) {\n        parse_status = absl::InvalidArgumentError(\"Invalid ALPN protocol string\");\n        return {};\n      }\n\n      out[start] = i - start;\n      start = i + 1;\n    } else {\n      out[i + 1] = alpn_protocols[i];\n    }\n  }\n\n  return out;\n}\n\nabsl::StatusOr<bssl::UniquePtr<SSL>>\nContextImpl::newSsl(const Network::TransportSocketOptionsConstSharedPtr& options) {\n  // We use the first certificate for a new SSL object, later in the\n  // SSL_CTX_set_select_certificate_cb() callback following ClientHello, we replace with the\n  // selected certificate via SSL_set_SSL_CTX().\n  auto ssl_con = bssl::UniquePtr<SSL>(SSL_new(tls_contexts_[0].ssl_ctx_.get()));\n  SSL_set_app_data(ssl_con.get(), &options);\n  return ssl_con;\n}\n\nenum ssl_verify_result_t ContextImpl::customVerifyCallback(SSL* ssl, uint8_t* out_alert) {\n  auto* extended_socket_info = reinterpret_cast<Envoy::Ssl::SslExtendedSocketInfo*>(\n      SSL_get_ex_data(ssl, ContextImpl::sslExtendedSocketInfoIndex()));\n  if (extended_socket_info->certificateValidationResult() != Ssl::ValidateStatus::NotStarted) {\n    if (extended_socket_info->certificateValidationResult() == Ssl::ValidateStatus::Pending) {\n      return ssl_verify_retry;\n    }\n    ENVOY_LOG(trace, \"Already has a result: {}\",\n              static_cast<int>(extended_socket_info->certificateValidationStatus()));\n    // Already has a binary result, return immediately.\n    *out_alert = extended_socket_info->certificateValidationAlert();\n    return extended_socket_info->certificateValidationResult() == Ssl::ValidateStatus::Successful\n               ? ssl_verify_ok\n               : ssl_verify_invalid;\n  }\n  // Hasn't kicked off any validation for this connection yet.\n  SSL_CTX* ssl_ctx = SSL_get_SSL_CTX(ssl);\n  ContextImpl* context_impl = static_cast<ContextImpl*>(SSL_CTX_get_app_data(ssl_ctx));\n  auto transport_socket_options_shared_ptr_ptr =\n      static_cast<const Network::TransportSocketOptionsConstSharedPtr*>(SSL_get_app_data(ssl));\n  ASSERT(transport_socket_options_shared_ptr_ptr);\n  ValidationResults result = context_impl->customVerifyCertChain(\n      extended_socket_info, *transport_socket_options_shared_ptr_ptr, ssl);\n  switch (result.status) {\n  case ValidationResults::ValidationStatus::Successful:\n    return ssl_verify_ok;\n  case ValidationResults::ValidationStatus::Pending:\n    return ssl_verify_retry;\n  case ValidationResults::ValidationStatus::Failed: {\n    if (result.tls_alert.has_value() && out_alert) {\n      *out_alert = result.tls_alert.value();\n    }\n    return ssl_verify_invalid;\n  }\n  }\n  PANIC(\"not reached\");\n}\n\nValidationResults ContextImpl::customVerifyCertChain(\n    Envoy::Ssl::SslExtendedSocketInfo* extended_socket_info,\n    const Network::TransportSocketOptionsConstSharedPtr& transport_socket_options, SSL* ssl) {\n  ASSERT(extended_socket_info);\n  STACK_OF(X509)* cert_chain = SSL_get_peer_full_cert_chain(ssl);\n  if (cert_chain == nullptr) {\n    extended_socket_info->setCertificateValidationStatus(Ssl::ClientValidationStatus::NotValidated);\n    stats_.fail_verify_error_.inc();\n    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"verify cert failed: no cert chain\");\n    return {ValidationResults::ValidationStatus::Failed, Ssl::ClientValidationStatus::NotValidated,\n            SSL_AD_INTERNAL_ERROR, absl::nullopt};\n  }\n  ASSERT(cert_validator_);\n  const char* host_name = SSL_get_servername(ssl, TLSEXT_NAMETYPE_host_name);\n\n  CertValidator::ExtraValidationContext validation_ctx;\n  validation_ctx.callbacks =\n      static_cast<Network::TransportSocketCallbacks*>(SSL_get_ex_data(ssl, sslSocketIndex()));\n\n extended_socket_info->setCertificateValidationStatus(result.detailed_status);\n    extended_socket_info->onCertificateValidationCompleted(\n        result.status == ValidationResults::ValidationStatus::Successful, false);\n  }\n  return result;\n}\n\nvoid ContextImpl::incCounter(const Stats::StatName name, absl::string_view value,\n ContextImpl::logHandshake(SSL* ssl) const {\n  stats_.handshake_.inc();\n\n  if (SSL_session_reused(ssl)) {\n    stats_.session_reused_.inc();\n  }\n\n  incCounter(ssl_ciphers_, absl::Status& parse_status) {\n  std::vector<uint8_t> parsed_alpn = parseAlpnProtocols(absl::StrJoin(alpn, \",\"), parse_status);\n  if (!parse_status.ok()) {\n    return false;\n  }\n  if const SSL_CIPHER* c = SSL_get_cipher_by_value(cipher_id);\n  if (c == nullptr) {\n    return false;\n  }\n  // Skip TLS 1.2 only ciphersuites unless the client supports it.\n  if (SSL_CIPHER_get_min_version(c) > client_version) {\n    return false;\n  }\n  if (SSL_CIPHER_get_auth_nid(c) != NID_auth_ecdsa) {\n    return false;\n  }\n  for (const SSL_CIPHER* our_c : SSL_CTX_get_ciphers(ssl_ctx_.get())) {\n    if (SSL_CIPHER_get_id(our_c) == SSL_CIPHER_get_id(c)) {\n      return true;\n    }\n  }\n  return false;\n}\n\nabsl::Status TlsContext::loadCertificateChain(const std::string& data,\n                                              const std::string& data_path) {\n  cert_chain_file_path_ = data_path;\n  bssl::UniquePtr<BIO> bio(BIO_new_mem_buf(const_cast<char*>(data.data()), data.size()));\n  RELEASE_ASSERT(bio != nullptr, \"\");\n  cert_chain_.reset(PEM_read_bio_X509_AUX(bio.get(), nullptr, nullptr, nullptr));\n  if (cert_chain_ == nullptr || !SSL_CTX_use_certificate(ssl_ctx_.get(), cert_chain_.get())) {\n    logSslErrorChain();\n    return absl::InvalidArgumentError(\n        absl::StrCat(\"Failed to load certificate chain from \", cert_chain_file_path_));\n  }\n  // Read rest of the certificate chain.\n  while (true) {\n    bssl::UniquePtr<X509> cert(PEM_read_bio_X509(bio.get(), nullptr, nullptr, nullptr));\n    if (cert == nullptr) {\n      break;\n    }\n    if (!SSL_CTX_add_extra_chain_cert(ssl_ctx_.get(), cert.get())) {\n      return absl::InvalidArgumentError(\n          absl::StrCat(\"Failed to load certificate chain from \", cert_chain_file_path_));\n    }\n    // SSL_CTX_add_extra_chain_cert() takes ownership.\n    cert.release();\n  }\n  // Check for EOF.\n  const uint32_t err = ERR_peek_last_error();\n  if (ERR_GET_LIB(err) == ERR_LIB_PEM && ERR_GET_REASON(err) == PEM_R_NO_START_LINE) {\n    ERR_clear_error();\n  } else {\n    return absl::InvalidArgumentError(\n        absl::StrCat(\"Failed to load certificate chain from \", cert_chain_file_path_));\n  }\n  return absl::OkStatus();\n}\n\nabsl::Status TlsContext::loadPrivateKey(const std::string& data, const std::string& data_path,\n                                        const std::string& password) {\n  bssl::UniquePtr<BIO> bio(BIO_new_mem_buf(const_cast<char*>(data.data()), data.size()));\n  RELEASE_ASSERT(bio != nullptr, \"\");\n  bssl::UniquePtr<EVP_PKEY> pkey(\n      PEM_read_bio_PrivateKey(bio.get(), nullptr, nullptr,\n                              !password.empty() ? const_cast<char*>(password.c_str()) : nullptr));\n\n  if (pkey == nullptr || !SSL_CTX_use_PrivateKey(ssl_ctx_.get(), pkey.get())) {\n    return absl::InvalidArgumentError(fmt::format(\n        \"Failed to load private key from {}, Cause: {}\", data_path,\n
